import requests

# URL Studentsite UG
url_ss = 'https://www.tempo.co/'
laman_ss = requests.get(url_ss)
# jika sukses, maka status query ini adalah 200, alias OK
print(f'Status GET laman SS UG: {laman_ss.status_code}')

Status GET laman SS UG: 200

# cetak HTML
print(laman_ss.content)

       <script type="text/javascript">
        (function (win, doc) {
          function mock(fn) {
              return function () {
                  this._.push([fn, arguments])
              }
          }

          function load(url) {
              const script = doc.createElement("script");
              script.type = "text/javascript";
              script.async = true;
              script.src = url;
              doc.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
          }

          win.remplib = win.remplib || {};
          const mockFuncs = {
              "campaign": "init",
              "tracker": "init trackEvent trackPageview trackCommerce",
              "iota": "init"
          };

          Object.keys(mockFuncs).forEach(function (key) {
              if (!win.remplib[key]) {
                  let fn, i, funcs = mockFuncs[key].split(" ");
                  win.remplib[key] = {_: []};

                  for (i = 0; i < funcs.length; i++) {
                      fn = funcs[i];
                      win.remplib[key][fn] = mock(fn);
                  }
              }
          });
          load("https://campaign.tempo.co/assets/lib/js/remplib.js");
          load("https://beam.tempo.co/assets/lib/js/remplib.js");
      })(window, document);

      // configuration
      // 
      const rempConfig = {
          token: "afb259bd-4c5e-410e-8c94-f109fbe3cb37",

          signedIn: false,          articleElement: document.getElementById("article"),
          articleElementFn: function () {
              return document.getElementById("article");
          },

          // optional, controls where cookies (UTM parameters of visit) are stored
          cookieDomain: ".tempo.co",

          // optional, controls which type of storage should be used by default (`local_storage` or `cookie`)
          // default is `local_storage`
          storage: "local_storage",

          // optional article details
           article: {
               id: "teco_", // optional
  			 // category: "super-truper-sekcia",

           },

          // required, Tracker API specific options
          tracker: {
              url: "https://tracker-beam.tempo.co",
              timeSpent: {
                  enabled: true
              },

              readingProgress: {
                  enabled: false,
                  interval: 5,
              },
          },

          // required, Campaign specific options
          campaign: {
              // required, URL host of REMP Campaign
              url: "https://campaign.tempo.co",

              // Additional params that will be appended links within displayed banner
              //
              // Key represents variable name, value should be defined as callback returning string response.

   var CaptchaCallback = function() {
      grecaptcha.render('g-recaptcha1', {'sitekey' : '6LcGRoIkAAAAAO2shGzSFo7NCxe1tj15fLKIiWHw'});
      grecaptcha.render('g-recaptcha2', {'sitekey' : '6LcGRoIkAAAAAO2shGzSFo7NCxe1tj15fLKIiWHw'});

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
$('#loginPost').on('submit',function(e){
  e.preventDefault();

  var username = $("#username").val();
	var password = $("#password").val();
	var response = grecaptcha.getResponse(0);

	if(username.length == "") {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Isi Email Sebagai Username Anda !'
    });

  } else if(password.length == "") {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Isi Kata Sandi Anda Dengan Benar !'
    });

  }else if(!response) {

		Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Captcha Belum Benar !'
    });

	}else {

    $.ajax({

      url: "https://www.tempo.co/loginuserteco",
      type: "POST",
      data: {
          "username": username,
          "password": password,
					"g-recaptcha-response": response
      },

      success:function(response){

				console.log(response);

        if (response.return == true) {

          Swal.fire({
						icon: 'success',
            // title: 'Login Berhasil!',
						title: 'Loading...',
            // text: 'Loading...',
            text: response.msg,
            timer: 3000,
            showCancelButton: false,
            showConfirmButton: false
          })
          .then (function() {
            window.location.href = "https://www.tempo.co";
          });

        } else {

          Swal.fire({
						icon: 'warning',
            // title: 'Login Gagal!',
						title: response.msg,
            text: 'silahkan coba lagi!'
          })
					.then (function() {
            window.location.href = "https://www.tempo.co";
          });

        }

        console.log(response);

      },

      error:function(response){

          Swal.fire({
						icon: 'error',
            title: 'Opps!',
            text: 'server error!'
          });

          console.log(response);

      }

    });

  }

});

});
  </script>
  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
$('#regisPost').on('submit',function(e){
  e.preventDefault();

  var nama = $("#nama").val();
	var email = $("#email").val();
	var atmail = email.indexOf("@");
	var dotmail = email.lastIndexOf(".");
	var password = $("#passuser").val();
	var repassword = $("#repassuser").val();
	var response = grecaptcha.getResponse(1);

	if(nama.length == "") {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Nama Wajib Diisi !'
    });

  } else if(email.length == "") {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Email Wajib Diisi !'
    });

  }else if(atmail<1 || dotmail<atmail+2 || dotmail+2>=email.length) {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Isi Email Dengan Benar !'
    });

  }else if(password.length == "") {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Kata Sandi Wajib Diisi !'
    });

  }else if(repassword.length == "") {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Ulangi Kata Sandi Anda !'
    });

  }else if(password != repassword) {

    Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Kata Sandi Tidak Sama Dengan Kata Sandi Ulang !'
    });

  }else if(!response) {

		Swal.fire({
      icon: 'warning',
      title: 'Oops...',
      text: 'Captcha Belum Benar !'
    });

	}else {

    $.ajax({

      url: "https://www.tempo.co/registeruserteco",
      type: "POST",
      data: {
          "nama": nama,
					"email" : email,
					"password" : password,
          "repassword": repassword,
					"g-recaptcha": response
      },

			success:function(response){
				console.log(response);
        if (response.return == true) {

          Swal.fire({
            icon: 'success',
            title: 'Loading ...',
            // title: response.msg,
						timer: 3000,
            text: response.msg,
            // text: 'Loading ...',
						showCancelButton: false,
						showConfirmButton: false
          }).then (function() {
            window.location.href = "https://www.tempo.co";
          });

          // $("#nama").val('');
          // $("#email").val('');
          // $("#password").val('');

        } else {

          Swal.fire({
            icon: 'error',
            title: response.msg,
            text: 'silahkan coba lagi!'
          });

        }

        console.log(response);

      },

      error:function(response){
          Swal.fire({
            type: 'error',
            title: 'Opps!',
            text: 'server error!'
          });
      }



    });

  }

});

});
  </script>

    adaptiveHeight: false,
    });

judul_list = []
ringkasan_list = []

for berita in kontainer_berita:
    for judul in berita.find_all('h2'):
        judul_string = judul.get_text()
        # buang spasi yang tidak diperlukan
        judul_rapi = ' '.join(str(judul_string).strip().split()) 
        print(judul_rapi)
        # append judul ke list
        judul_list.append(judul_rapi)

    for rangkuman in berita.find_all('p'):
        rangkuman_rapi = ' '.join(str(rangkuman.get_text()).strip().split())
        print(rangkuman_rapi)
        # append teks rangkuman ke list
        ringkasan_list.append(rangkuman_rapi)
